mysql> SELECT title.f
    -> FROM film f
    -> ^C
mysql> SELECT f.title
    -> FROM film f
    ->  INNER JOIN actor a
    -> FROM^C
mysql> SELECT f.title
    -> FROM film f
    ->  INNER JOIN film_actor fa
    ->  ON f.film_id = fa.film_id
    ->  INNER JOIN actor a
    ->  ON fa.actor_id = a.actor_id
    -> WHERE a.first_name = 'John';
